. forvalues i=1/5 {
  2. tab hp`i'ownrentot 
  3. replace ownhome=hp`i'ownrentot==1 if wave==`i' & (!missing(hp`i'ownrento) | res_care==1)
  4. replace rent=hp`i'ownrentot==2 if wave==`i' & (!missing(hp`i'ownrento) | res_care==1)
  5. tab hp`i'mrtpadoff 
  6. replace mortgagepaidoff=hp`i'mrtpadoff==1 if !missing(hp`i'mrtpadoff)
  7. replace paysmortgage=hp`i'mrtpadoff==2 if !missing(hp`i'mrtpadoff)
  8. tab hp`i'mortpaymt 
  9. replace mortpaymt= hp`i'mortpaymt if wave==`i'
 10. qui replace mortpaymt=1 if wave==`i' & hp`i'mthlymort<250
 11. qui replace mortpaymt=2 if wave==`i' & hp`i'mthlymort>=250 & hp`i'mthlymort<=499
 12. qui replace mortpaymt=3 if wave==`i' & hp`i'mthlymort>=500 & hp`i'mthlymort<1000
 13. qui replace mortpaymt=4 if wave==`i' & hp`i'mthlymort>=1000 & !missing(hp`i'mthlymort)
 14. tab hp`i'whnpayoff 
 15. replace timeinmort=hp`i'whnpayoff if wave==`i'
 16. tab hp`i'amoutowed 
 17. replace owedonmort=hp`i'amoutowed if wave==`i'
 18. qui replace owedonmort=1 if wave==`i' & hp`i'amtstlowe<50000 
 19. qui replace owedonmort=2 if wave==`i' & hp`i'amtstlowe>=50000 & hp`i'amtstlowe<=100000
 20. qui replace owedonmort=3 if wave==`i' & hp`i'amtstlowe>=100000 & !missing(hp`i'amtstlowe)
 21. tab hp`i'homvalamt 
 22. replace homevalue= hp`i'homvalamt if wave==`i'
 23. qui replace homevalue=1 if wave==`i' & hp`i'homevalue<50000 & hp`i'homevalue>=0
 24. qui replace homevalue=2 if wave==`i' & hp`i'homevalue>=50000 & hp`i'homevalue<75000
 25. qui replace homevalue=3 if wave==`i' & hp`i'homevalue>=75000 & hp`i'homevalue<100000
 26. qui replace homevalue=4 if wave==`i' & hp`i'homevalue>=100000 & hp`i'homevalue<200000
 27. qui replace homevalue=5 if wave==`i' & hp`i'homevalue>=200000 & hp`i'homevalue<300000
 28. qui replace homevalue=6 if wave==`i' & hp`i'homevalue>=300000 & hp`i'homevalue<500000
 29. qui replace homevalue=7 if wave==`i' & hp`i'homevalue>=500000 & hp`i'homevalue<750000
 30. qui replace homevalue=8 if wave==`i' & hp`i'homevalue>=750000 & !missing(hp`i'homevalue)
 31. 
. tab hp`i'rentamou 
 32. replace rentpaid =hp`i'rentamou if wave==`i'
 33. qui replace rentpaid=1 if wave==`i' & hp`i'rentamt<250 & hp`i'rentamt>=0
 34. qui replace rentpaid=2 if wave==`i' & hp`i'rentamt>=250 & hp`i'rentamt<=499
 35. qui replace rentpaid=3 if wave==`i' & hp`i'rentamt>=500 & hp`i'rentamt<1000
 36. qui replace rentpaid=4 if wave==`i' & hp`i'rentamt>=1000 & !missing(hp`i'rentamt)
 37. qui replace rentpaid=4 if inlist(rentpaid,5,6)
 38. replace mortpaymt=4 if inlist(mortpaymt,5,6)
 39. tab hp1sec8pubsn
 40. replace section8=hp`i'sec8pubsn==1 if wave==`i' & (!missing(hp`i'sec8pubsn) |ownhome==1 | rent==1)
 41. }

. label var finhlpfam "Received financial help/gifts from family"

. gen n_social_network=.
(41,466 missing values generated)

. forvalues i=1/6 {
  2.         replace n_social_network=sn`i'dnumsn if sn`i'dnumsn>=0 & wave==`i'
  3. }
(7,026 real changes made)

(4,884 real changes made)

(7,093 real changes made)
(6,002 real changes made)

. label var n_social_network "Number in social network"

. 
. //and now drop all raw variables
. forvalues i=1/6 {
  2.         drop r`i'* ip`i'* is`i'* re`i'* hc`i'* ht`i'* hh`i'* ss`i'* fl`i'* ///
>          pc`i'* cp`i'* cg`i'* mo`i'* ha`i'* sc`i'* mc`i'* pa`i'* sd`i'* hw`i'* ///
>          cm`i'* sn`i'* hp`i'* ew`i'* ir`i'*
  3. }

. 
. drop el1* rl1* ia1* pd2* pd3* pd4* ia3* ia5*

. 
. rename round*status r*status

. 
. svyset varunit [pw=anfinwgt], strat(varstrat)

      pweight: anfinwgt
          VCE: linearized

     Strata 1: varstrat
         SU 1: varunit
        FPC 1: <zero>
